A Young Woman's Loss of Virtue

A Page from the History of Urban Crime

After Defiling Her, They Deceived Her of Her Possessions

The Punishment of the Three Young Men Seems Still Insufficient

Kuang Yue'e, a young woman from Changzhou, 26 years old, with a beautiful appearance, had been living in her hometown. Recently, because her husband, Xu Shengfu, had been working as a merchant in Shanghai for a long time without any news, his survival uncertain, out of longing, she prepared her luggage on the 2nd of this month and came to Shanghai alone to inquire about him. She stayed at the home of Ye Shitian at No. 7 Yude Lane, Yunnan Road, who had previously been a neighbor. Ye's profession was singing Suzhou ballads, and he had to go to the Ren Shi Jie amusement park to perform every day. Yue'e had long admired the prosperity of Shanghai. Although she had not yet found her husband, her mood and interest were not diminished. Therefore, she often followed Ye to the amusement park to enjoy the sights. Unexpectedly, she was

Targeted by Those Who Hunt for Beauty

They teased her incessantly. The woman's heart was not made of stone, and her feelings were stirred. One evening, she was lured by Zhu A'san, Liu Zhengyun, and Xiang Baoxian to the Qichang Hotel at the intersection of Hankou Road and Zhejiang Road for a deep conversation. However, it was difficult for three men and one woman to stay together. After Zhu and the others agreed amongst themselves, Zhu alone accompanied the woman to sleep, while Liu and Xiang left. As the beautiful morning dream was still deep, a woman named Shen, claiming to be Zhu's wife, suddenly knocked on the door, scolding Zhu for not cherishing his own wife and tasting wild flavors. They quarreled with each other. Yue'e, witnessing the scene,

Could Not Help But Feel Ashamed

She got up to leave. Zhu, knowing that Liu and Xiang were still hoping to get a share, transferred Yue'e to them. At that time, Liu happened to arrive. Yue'e saw that he was dressed in a Western suit, with a suave manner. The shame in her heart immediately dissipated, and she felt a sense of joy. From then on, she and Liu were together day and night. A few days ago, Liu said that he was going to Hangzhou for a spring outing and asked the woman to go with him. The woman immediately agreed. Liu then retrieved the luggage that she had left at Ye's house and brought it back to the hotel, and also asked Zhu and Shen to help move it. After the luggage was retrieved, Liu said to the woman again, "Your hairstyle is too old-fashioned and lacks elegance. I would like to accompany you to the barber shop

To Redo Your Hair."

At this time, the woman's mind had been completely seduced. She obeyed Liu's every command. They went straight to a barber shop on Wuma Road. As the hairdressing was only half finished, Liu suddenly claimed that the train to Hangzhou was about to depart. "Your hair is not yet completely cut, so I have to go buy the ticket first. I will definitely wait for you at the station." After saying this, he turned and left. Yue'e wanted to chase him but could not. After her hair was finished, she rushed back to the hotel, but all her luggage had disappeared. Because the hotel porter Huang Yuansheng had previously praised Liu for

How Wealthy He Was

She thought that Huang must know the whereabouts of Liu and the others, so she quickly inquired. However, Huang blamed the woman for being careless. Therefore, the woman reported to the Lao Zha police station, and detectives Wang Shusen and Cao Qishan investigated. Suspecting Huang Yuansheng, they arrested him. Based on Huang's confession, they rushed to No. 178 Luxiangyuan Road in the city and apprehended Zhu and Shen. After Shen confessed, they learned where Zhu and the others were hiding. They went to Room 138 of the Tongshang Hotel on Avenue Edward VII and recovered the original stolen suitcase. Then, they went to Room 11 of the Beiyang Hotel on Huaxing Road in Zhabei and arrested Zhu, Liu, and Xiang. The woman's belongings,

Clothing and Land Deeds

Etc., only a gold wristwatch and a diamond ring had been pawned. These have now been retrieved from the pawnshop. The remaining items are generally not missing, but her integrity has been completely destroyed. Yesterday morning, the police escorted Zhu and the others to the First Special District District Court. Judge Feng conducted the trial. The police lawyer Ru Baoyi stated the facts of the case and requested that the defendants be punished according to the crime of theft. Kuang Yue'e recounted the process of being seduced. Judge Feng then questioned each of the defendants one by one. In conclusion, Huang Yuansheng was found not guilty. Zhu, Liu, and Xiang were each sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment. The stolen goods were returned to the original owner.

Poisoning from Eating Sea Snails

| Director Wu of the Health Bureau Discusses the Reasons |

A few days ago, the owner of the Yi Hong Yuan brothel on Dongxinqiao Street in the French Concession purchased a large batch of sea snails to distribute to the prostitutes in the brothel to celebrate the summer solstice festival on the lunar calendar. Because the purchased snails were particularly large, the prostitutes competed to eat them. Unexpectedly, thirteen of the prostitutes suddenly fell ill the day after eating them, suffering from headaches, fever, abdominal pain, and loss of appetite, leading to suspicions of poisoning. Fortunately, there were no fatalities. After the reporter went to investigate, they obtained several leftover sea snails.

Director Wu Liguo's Explanation

Yesterday, I visited Wu Liguo, the director of the Second Section of the Municipal Health Bureau, and told him the whole story. According to him, sea snails are a type of hard-shelled food. If people with weak digestive systems eat too much, it is very easy to get sick. Moreover, sea snails may have decayed or grown bacteria inside the shell due to prolonged exposure, making them very dangerous to eat.

What People in the Fishing Industry Said

The reporter also visited people in the fishing industry to investigate the origin of sea snails. According to them, they are produced in the sandy mudflats along the coast. They can be picked up everywhere when the tide recedes. However, it is safe to eat small ones before the summer solstice, but particularly large ones should not be eaten after the summer solstice. There is a type of red dragonfly in summer that cannot be eaten. It is said that this red dragonfly is transformed from this type of particularly large sea snail. However, it is unlikely that a shelled animal can transform into a winged animal.

The Thirteen Are Fortunately Unharmed

Fortunately, all thirteen prostitutes in the brothel were unharmed after eating the snails. According to their careful observation, a suspicious point was discovered: after these large sea snails were soaked and cooked in hot water, tiny green spots appeared in the gaps in their shells, while ordinary small sea snails did not show this change even after being soaked and cooked in hot water. Wei Sheng, 32 years old, from Jiading; Zhang Zhixing, 41 years old, from Shanghai; Qin Axiang, 35 years old, from Wuxi; and Zhu Jinlin, 39 years old, from Shanghai, were arrested. The remaining principals, including Jin Bao and Detective Li from a certain place, escaped and have not yet been apprehended. They were all taken into custody along with the team and presented for investigation. However, it was learned yesterday that the four arrested were not serious offenders and have reportedly been released after paying a fine.

Tu Wenzhao Agrees to Move Contraband Fish

The Every Day News reports that after the Municipal Fisheries Inspection Committee discovered that the Japanese fishing boat Kaiyo Maru No. 9 was importing large quantities of contraband fish, which were being stored in the Hongchang Cold Storage Company's cold storage on Miller Road, in addition to submitting the case to the first meeting of the Municipal Fisheries Association's directors and supervisors for handling, they also submitted a request to the Social Bureau yesterday to prevent the company from registering. After the Fisheries Association issued a warning, the company has moved the contraband fish. The details are recorded below:

Report to the Social Bureau

Report Regarding Japanese Vessels' Infringement on Fishing Rights and the Hongchang Cold Storage Company's Collusion by Storing Contraband Fish; Requesting that Registration be Denied. It has come to our Association's attention on the 3rd of this month that the Japanese fishing boat Kaiyo Maru has caught over 3,000 boxes of yellow croaker and other fish in our Zhejiang waters, and is freezing them in the Hongchang Cold Storage Company on Miller Road in the Public Concession, falsely claiming that they were caught by Chinese fishermen, which is a severe infringement on our national rights. The Hongchang Cold Storage Company has not been open for long and specializes in cold-storing fresh and salted fish and other goods for the Japanese, hoping to profit from this. It is now learned that the company is planning to register with your Bureau to facilitate its business. Therefore, our Association has exposed this scheme and submitted it to the second joint meeting of directors and supervisors for deliberation, requesting that your Bureau deny the company's registration (remainder omitted).

Fisheries Association Warning

According to the decision made at the first meeting of directors and supervisors on the 7th, the Municipal Fisheries Association dispatched representatives Huang Zhenshi and Wang Yunpu to the company yesterday morning at 11:00 AM, along with personnel from the Fisheries Guidance Office. They met with Manager Tu Wenzhao and explained the greater picture to him, urging him to quickly move the stored contraband fish. Manager Tu Wenzhao replied that he had already negotiated with Jiang Azhen, the original handler, and that the stored contraband fish would be completely moved out within the next two days. He also stated that he would no longer trade with the Japanese in the future and was willing to publish a public announcement in the newspaper to clarify his intentions.

Be Careful of Dogs Poisoned with Spurge Laurel

Recently, there have been reports of people in Shanghai poisoning dogs. Twelve dogs have died so far. It is now learned that these individuals are active again. They use spurge laurel wrapped in meat, throwing it into fences or next to houses, paying particular attention to Danish Great Danes. Dog owners must take strong precautions. When dogs are idle, they should wear muzzles. If suspicious individuals are seen loitering near the house, they should be questioned. If pieces of meat are found in the yard, they should be reported to the police station immediately. If a dog swallows poison, it should be given a weight-based emetic immediately. For Danish dogs, use one tablespoon of table salt dissolved in warm water and drench the dog with it. If the dog is smaller, reduce the amount of salt accordingly. Drench the dog as much as possible to ensure that the meat is vomited out and the poison is not absorbed into the body. After the dog vomits, drench it with a mixture of one part brandy and three parts water. Place the dog in a dark, quiet place and wait for the veterinarian to arrive.

The Melon Seed King Involved in a Lawsuit

"Delicious" Sues "Fortune, Prosperity, and Longevity" for Counterfeiting

Sold in Various Tea and Snack Shops

Rong Songnian, a native of Ningbo, runs a certain Japanese shop in Rongji Lane, Wuma Road, and has been making huge profits over the years. Two years ago, he invested 5,000 yuan to establish the "Delicious" company, imitating Ningbo's Dayou soy sauce melon seeds. In less than half a year, he made a profit of 50,000 to 60,000 yuan. Because he did not distribute bonuses to his colleagues according to the regulations, the capable staff resigned one after another and formed the "Fortune, Prosperity, and Longevity" company, whose business is booming and sales are very wide. Rong was jealous and filed a criminal lawsuit against Du Chuqing, an employee of the "Fortune, Prosperity, and Longevity" company, for the crime of counterfeiting trademarks. The case was heard yesterday in the Fifth Criminal Division of the First District Court. Rong appeared in court and claimed that the defendant had counterfeited his "King" trademark. Du also appeared in court with his lawyer, and each presented their trademarks for inspection. The plaintiff's trademark was a "lonely crane," while the defendant's trademark was a "three stars," with no similarity at all. The plaintiff then stated that the words "King" in the phrase "Melon Seed King" had been registered for patent. The defendant argued that the plaintiff had not used the words "King" as a trademark. He then presented the plaintiff's melon seed bag as evidence, stating that "Melon Seed King" is a common and ordinary food name, sold in various tea and snack shops (and presented melon seed bags from various shops for verification), and there is no possibility of patent. There is a clear distinction between the trademark "King" and the name "Melon Seed King." Furthermore, the "Fortune, Prosperity, and Longevity" company has a manager responsible, and he is not responsible for anything. Now the plaintiff must know that the manager of the "Fortune, Prosperity, and Longevity" company is his uncle but does not sue him, deliberately slandering him. He immediately filed a counterclaim for the crime of malicious prosecution. After the lawyers on both sides debated the matter, because it was late, it was announced that the trial would be continued on the 15th.

Ji Shan Xuan About to Relocate

Ji Shan Xuan was founded by people from Haining and is organized by philanthropic gentlemen from Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. It specializes in distributing prescriptions, summer medicine, and other pills and powders needed for various ailments at Gujia Lane, Ningbo Road, Shanghai. It has been operating this charitable cause for fifteen years. Countless poor people have benefited from the Xuan. The expenses required are all donated by members according to their ability. Since the impact of the January 28th Incident, members have been scattered. In order to save expenses, the Haining natives moved the Xuan to the fourth floor of a certain building in Wu Shao Lane. Recently, due to the inconvenience of going in and out, in response to the request of the majority of members, they have leased No. 17 Xiangfen Lane as an office. It is currently being renovated. It is said that the renovation will be completed soon, and they plan to move in and continue to carry out various charitable activities as usual.

Pan Zhongce

Commits Suicide by Poison Due to Economic Hardship

Rescued by Doctors and Granted a New Life

Relapses with a Severe Illness and Finally Passes Away

Pan Zhongce, a native of Jiaxing, Zhejiang, was 23 years old this year and not yet married. He had parents and a six-year-old younger brother at home. Pan used to work in the rice business in Shanghai, but recently he became unemployed, resulting in economic hardship. He suddenly had suicidal thoughts. At 3:00 PM on the 5th of this month, he went alone to the Anle Second Hotel at No. 4 Aide Lane, Zhengjia Muqiao Street, in the French Concession and rented Room 33. After entering the room, he closed the door tightly and wrote two suicide notes. He took poison that night and the poison took effect in the middle of the night. The room attendant discovered him and reported it to the front desk. The police were notified and sent Pan to Renji Hospital for treatment. The suicide notes were taken back to the police station and filed. Pan entered the hospital and was rescued by doctors, who removed the poison, and he was granted a new life. However, because his body had undergone a major blow, he was mentally exhausted and remained in the hospital for treatment. Unexpectedly, his condition worsened. The treatment was ineffective, and he died at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday. The hospital notified the police, who sent a detective to the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home to examine the body. No family members were found, and a report was filed with the Second Special District Court yesterday. Prosecutor Deng Baosun was commissioned to go to the funeral home and verified that the deceased had died of illness. The case was officially closed. Room attendant Lu Chunkun was questioned about the circumstances of the discovery, and the detectives presented the suicide notes. The official then ordered the body to be photographed and buried by the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home, awaiting identification by relatives.

Young Woman Cries Uncontrollably After Taking Poison

Dies After Being Sent to Bao Long Hospital

Commits Suicide After Failing to Stop Husband from Gambling

The woman Wu Song, from Ningbo, was 19 years old and of good appearance. Her husband, Wu Qingrong, worked at the Jinye Exchange. Usually, the couple were very harmonious and lived in a certain place on Laoshenjiao Road in the French Concession. Recently, she had given birth to a child, so she was in poor health. A few days ago, she returned to her mother's house at No. 232 Bao'an Lane, Tianjin Road, to recuperate. Her husband also temporarily resided there. The day before yesterday, when Wu Gongbi returned, he told his wife that friends had invited him to gamble. The woman believed that gambling was a way to waste money and energy, so she advised him not to go. Unexpectedly, her husband refused to listen, which led to an argument. After Wu left, the woman was very upset and suddenly had the idea of ending her life. She swallowed opium and tried to kill herself. When her husband returned home, it was already late at 11:00 PM. He saw his wife lying on the bed, her face pale, crying uncontrollably. After questioning her repeatedly, he learned that she had taken poison. He immediately sent her to Bao Long Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and she soon died. The hospital reported to the Lao Zha police station, and Detective Qiu Sijiu was ordered to investigate. He carried the body to the Verifying Body Office on Ferry Road. Yesterday morning, the First Special District District Court commissioned Prosecutor Guo Wei to go to the office and verify the body. The case was officially closed. According to the statement of the deceased's husband, Wu Qingrong, the deceased was his wife. She was usually quiet and reserved. The day before yesterday, because he could not refuse the invitation of friends, he went out to play mahjong. She wanted to stop him from going, which led to a slight argument. Unexpectedly, she committed suicide by taking poison because of this trivial matter. Guo heard the statement and ruled that the deceased, Wu Song, had died from opium poisoning. The body was handed over to her husband, Wu Qingrong, who made a guarantee to take it back for burial. The Perpetrators in the Xiaoshan Kidnapping Case Sentenced

Shen Yun, a Shaoxing native who committed kidnapping, in February of this year, under the order of the fugitive bandit leader Shen Chuan Dog, gathered more than ten fellow villagers, including Zhang Baichuan, Wang A'chang, Lu Shangao, Zhou Chuanfu, and Liu Xichen, and went to the Tongshanwan village in Xiaoshan County, Shaoxing, and kidnapped Chen Zurong, the fourteen-year-old only son of Chen Tianyou's family, and brought him to Shanghai. They hid him in the home of fellow villager Chen Shiying at No. 3 Ping'an Lane, Xuehuali Road, in the French Concession. They demanded a large ransom from the victim. On the afternoon of March 10th, they arranged for the victim to meet at the Yuli entrance on Caishi Street to discuss the ransom. The French Concession Police Special Agent Jin Jiulin learned of this and led the detectives Zhang Ziquan, Zhou Bingcheng, and Zhou Yaoting, along with patrol officers, to rush to the scene. They arrested Shen and the others, along with suspects Gao Bin, Chen Sheng, Wu Wang, Wang Chen, and Chuan Lanying, a total of twelve men and women. The victim was rescued, and they were sent to the Second Special District Court. The police lawyer filed a public prosecution in accordance with Article 1, Section 1, of the Law on the Punishment of Bandits. The interrogation details have been reported previously. The case has now been concluded. Yesterday, Judge Li Changnian presided over the criminal court and ordered the defendants to be brought to court. Shen Yun was sentenced to 18 years in prison for kidnapping and extortion, and deprived of his civil rights for 18 years. Zhang Baichuan, Wang A'chang, Lu Shangao, Zhou Chuanfu, and Liu Xichen were each sentenced to 15 years in prison for kidnapping and extortion, and deprived of their civil rights for 15 years. Chen Shiying was sentenced to 12 years in prison for assisting in kidnapping and extortion, and deprived of his civil rights for 12 years. The number of days of detention before the judgment was confirmed was calculated at two days to one day of imprisonment. Gao Bin, Chen Sheng, Wang Chen, Wu Wang, and Chuan Lanying were all found not guilty. During the appeal period, Shen and the other seven were detained in the detention center. Gao and the other five were released on bail. Those without bail were detained.

Englishman's Car Runs Over a Boy

Yang Yongliang, the six-year-old son of Yang Xiaoxun, a native of Dabu, Guangdong, who lived at No. 751 Minquan Road in the French Concession, was led by his grandmother past No. 301 Avenue Edward VII at 1:00 PM on the 6th of this month. While crossing the road from south to north, a private car No. 11658 driven by a driver hired by a British man named Pete was coming from the east heading west. They were unable to avoid each other, and the child was knocked down by the fender and injured his head. The police arrived and sent the injured child to Renji Hospital for treatment. The driver was taken to the police station to await instructions. The child died of his injuries on the evening of the 8th. The police sent the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home. Yesterday, the Traffic Department reported to the Second Special District Court, and Prosecutor Deng was commissioned to go to the funeral home, verified the body, and officially opened the case. The defendant, the driver, was questioned about the circumstances of the accident. The official ruled that Yang Yongliang had died of injuries caused by a car accident. The body was taken by the family for burial. The defendant was returned to the Traffic Department for questioning.

Our Company

The Sale of Golden Goblet Champagne Tickets Will End on a Fixed Date

Since our company began selling Golden Goblet Champagne tickets for Henan, Anhui, and Hubei provinces, purchases have been very enthusiastic, and the remaining tickets are few. The drawing date has been extended to June 3rd, and the time is very short. Our company has now decided to end the sale on the 25th of this month in advance. Letters from other places purchasing tickets that arrive in Shanghai after the 25th will have their money returned immediately. Those who wish to purchase tickets should do so quickly.

National Humiliation Week Speech

Mr. Zhang Yousan's View on Sino-Japanese Relations

May 7th at the Shanghai YMCA

Ladies and gentlemen, today is the first day of National Humiliation Commemoration Week. May has always been a month of many disasters, and many National Humiliation Days, such as May 3rd, May 7th, and May 9th, are especially related to Japan. During this time of national crisis, commemorating national humiliation is naturally very sad and indignant; but in the midst of grief, we should think about how to cope with this national crisis. Now that time is short, I will briefly say a few words.

The current proposals for coping with the national crisis can be roughly divided into five points: first, war, that is, declaring war on Japan; second, peace, that is, negotiating peace with Japan; third, struggle, that is, long-term resistance; fourth, reliance, that is, relying on international forces to sanction Japan; and fifth, delay, that is, not adopting any measures, but simply delaying the time. Now I will briefly analyze these five proposals.

(1) Pro-War. Now Japan is carrying out various forms of violent aggression. The atrocities of September 18th and January 28th, as well as the loss of Jehol, have only increased. This has aroused the emotions of the Chinese people to the extreme. Of course, no one wants to be subjected to humiliation, and everyone wants to use force to deal with it. Anyone with blood in their veins has this idea. Therefore, we often hear calls for declarations of war and severance of relations. From the perspective of emotions and blood alone, absolutely no one opposes this pro-war approach, but we must analyze its advantages and disadvantages. The first advantage of the pro-war approach is that once a formal war begins, it can allow the general public's indignant emotions to be vented. Although the sacrifices of war are great, we are willing to sacrifice, because enduring the current suffocating suffering is really more unbearable than a quick and painful sacrifice. Second, it can maintain the nation's dignity. Given China's current situation, enduring all kinds of oppression while still swallowing insults makes it really difficult to gain a foothold in the world. If we declare war on Japan, regardless of victory or defeat, at least we can win back some dignity for the country. Third, external resistance may promote internal unity in China. The country is still divided. If we declare war on the outside, even if we cannot unite wholeheartedly, at least all parties will not dare to openly squabble. Fourth, declaring war can change the international atmosphere. The diplomatic policies of various countries can shift depending on the strength of our country's resistance. China is currently a great sales market for the world's advanced industrial countries. If China and Japan declare war, it will inevitably jeopardize their commercial relations, and they will have to come forward to intervene. Especially Britain and the United States have the deepest relationship with the Far East. The Yangtze River basin is entirely within the British sphere of influence. Once it is affected, the British will inevitably step in. All these can be caused by war to motivate the world to jointly sanction Japan. These five reasons for pro-war are of course theoretical. In reality, is it difficult to declare war? Those who advocate not going to war believe that declaring war on Japan is impossible. There are five reasons. (A) No Weapons of War. Although China's army has about three million soldiers, the number is not small, but there is a great lack of modern weapons of war. We know that modern warfare cannot be done without relying on modern weapons. The navy is especially pathetic. The total tonnage of all the warships in the country is only 30,000 tons. In terms of air force, although all walks of life are now promoting aviation to save the country, it is impossible to say whether it will be effective. We often see in the newspapers that there are broadsword teams in the north, repeatedly defeating powerful enemies in the northeast. Their brave spirit is naturally worthy of our twelve points of admiration, but to say that a body of flesh and blood, relying on a knife, can compete with airplanes, bombs, and tanks is something that anyone with a little common sense will know is difficult to do in reality. (B) No Military Discipline. To fight a foreign war, command must be unified and orders must be obeyed. Now the northern armies fighting are not closely linked, and they are fighting on their own. One side is experiencing very tense battles, while the other side stands by and watches, as if it has nothing to do with them. For example, when the battle of Jehol was recently tense, only Sun Dianying, Song Zheyuan, etc. were fighting hard along the Great Wall, while most of the others were standing still. With such a battle, how much chance of victory is there? (C) No Diplomacy. Modern international warfare cannot be fought in isolation with one country against others. Which country in the world can stand on the same side as us now? Without diplomatic coordination, there is absolutely no hope of victory. (D) No Relief. Military supplies and transportation are very important in the military. China's industry and transportation have no foundation. Even petroleum, an indispensable item in wartime, would cause panic if the source of petroleum were cut off once the sea lanes were blockaded, even if there were airplanes and tanks, they would have to be parked and unable to move. Also, copper, iron, sulfuric acid, nitric acid, hydrochloric acid, and all kinds of machinery are all dependent on foreign countries, and transportation stoppages will cause panic. The lack of food is also a problem. (E) The People Are Not Organized. Now, if we want to fight Japan, we must mobilize the whole country. If the people lack organizational ability, the outcome of the front is not yet determined, and the rear is already in turmoil. This is also an obstacle to warfare. In summary, the general public believes that the outcome of going to war with Japan is not certain. (2) Pro-Peace. Since September 18th, no one wanted peace, and no one dared to talk about peace, but now, because the Japanese are pressing into Shanhaiguan and some people in the north have begun to openly discuss peace. Their proposal is to abandon the regions outside Shanhaiguan in order to preserve Tianjin and Beiping. However, peace must have conditions. The conditions for peace: (1) If the two countries are evenly matched, and once a dispute arises, the outcome of victory or defeat is not yet determined, in order to avoid both sides suffering, it is best to make peace. In this case, peace is possible; (2) If one of the two countries is first defeated and then turns into a small victory, and the situation has turned, it is better to make peace at this time than to surrender under duress. In this case, peace is also possible; (3) If the two countries are in a stalemate and a third strong country comes out to intervene, then peace can also be made, because both sides are under pressure, and one side will not suffer excessive losses; (4) If one of the two countries, the victor, is already exhausted and willing to end the war, and the defeated side makes peace at this time, it will not suffer great losses. In this case, peace is also possible. These are the four conditions under which peace is possible. Now that we want to make peace, do we have these four conditions? Of course, we don't have any of them. So how can we make peace? Even if we take a step back, peace should have been discussed at the very beginning of the September 18th Incident. At that time, there was still the possibility of opening negotiations. Now that the four provinces have already been occupied and are about to encroach on Tianjin and Beiping, if we go to make peace with Japan at this time, that is simply surrendering under duress. And even if we abandon the Northeast and use the Great Wall as the boundary to seek temporary peace, can we satisfy the Japanese desire? This is probably impossible! The Japanese ambition for the mainland is extremely great. They will not be satisfied unless they completely annex our country. They not only have this ambition for our country, but also want to sweep up the territories of Britain and the United States in East Asia. Speaking like this, the road to peace is absolutely impossible. And at this time, absolutely no one dares to openly bear the responsibility of making peace, so peace cannot be achieved. (3) Pro-Struggle. Struggle means long-term resistance. If there is no power to declare war, change the strategy to exhaust the enemy and cause internal collapse. Although this method is not as extensive as a formal declaration of war, equipment command relief, etc. should also be well prepared, which refers to our resistance. As for the Japanese invasion, the new budget of the Japanese government, the income for this year is 1.28 billion yuan, and the expenditure is 2.23 billion yuan, which is tens of millions of yuan in arrears, of which the navy and army expenses account for 800 million yuan. This is Japan's expense. The total Japanese national debt is 6.3 billion yuan, and each citizen must bear an average of 100 yuan. From this point of view, Japan's internal collapse is not impossible. In short, Japan's domestic economy is tight, which is undeniable. But for this reason, they are eagerly seizing the Northeast in order to solve the economic difficulties, so they regard the Northeast as a lifeline. The three northeastern provinces are rich in products, such as timber, soybeans, steel, coal, placer gold, livestock, grains, etc. The income is not low. Once developed by the Japanese, it will be an unlimited source of wealth. The customs tax revenue in the 20th year of the Republic was 26 million taels, and the salt tax was 19 million taels. Since the Japanese have obtained the above, they can slightly relieve the economic panic and implement mass immigration. Japan is now experiencing rural bankruptcy and worker unemployment. There is unrest everywhere. The original situation was precarious, but since winning the war, they have made every effort to publicize and anesthetize the people, which is quite enough to increase the people's belief in the government. The Japanese army sent to the Northeast is only about 50,000 people, about 3 or more divisions, which is enough to run amok, while the people of our country are suffering endless torture. So to say that struggle is not effective in the near future. (4) Pro-Reliance, that is, relying on other countries to come out and help us, and using force to stop the violent Japanese. This is the worst policy, and the relationship between international relations is complicated and confusing. It is a pipe dream to want them to speak with force now. There are several points in the current international situation that are beneficial to Japan: (A) Capitalist countries want the Japanese to be the vanguard of the anti-Russian front, and they are not willing to offend Japan. (B) Western European countries are competing for dominance, and some countries, such as France, want to obtain assistance in the international arena and are trying to win over Japan. (C) The economies of various countries are declining and they are unable to take care of international sanctions. (D) The interests of major countries such as Britain and the United States still have some conflicts, and their steps cannot be coordinated. Recently, there is a possibility of rapprochement between Britain, the United States, and France at the Washington Conference, but it is still feared that Japan will feign pro-Russian relations to make threats. In this situation, it is difficult for Europe and the United States to use force to sanction Japan. Even if any country comes out, it will be of no benefit to our country. It is nothing more than a competition for markets. (5) Pro-Delay. That is to delay time. This is the method that is currently being implemented. We are just passing the days casually. Of course, this is the worst method, and it cannot be considered a method. But now that war is impossible, peace is unacceptable, struggle is unfeasible, and reliance is unreliable, some people can only use delay as the only solution in a situation where nothing is possible. In this impossible situation, what should we do? We need to look further. We should regard the trauma we have suffered as a lesson. If we can learn from this lesson and make efforts to revive ourselves, there is still a glimmer of hope for the future. Otherwise, our country will truly be doomed forever. Since the Sino-Japanese War, how many times has Japan invaded our country? We should have realized all these stimuli long ago. But the Chinese people are too unwilling to be competitive. The stimuli are repeated over and over again, but we just let them pass, so the invasion is getting worse every time. If we can carefully examine the reasons for being invaded, which stem from our own corruption, then to fundamentally save ourselves, we still need to revitalize the spirit of our nation. Currently, there are only two ways to cope with the national crisis: one is to treat the symptoms, and the other is to treat the root cause. The way to treat the symptoms is to continue to make every effort to resist, and there must be more powerful resistance. The increase in military equipment, the unity of command, the relief of material, and the diplomatic efforts are all necessary conditions for resistance. In terms of treating the root cause, we hope that the government will be responsible for handling four items: (1) The livelihood of the people. Now the people are living in poverty, which must be resolved urgently. (2) Safeguarding civil rights. The basic rights of the people, such as personal, speech, and freedom of association, must be guaranteed. (3) Purify officialdom and severely punish corruption. (4) Prepare national defense. What is hoped for from the people is the revitalization of their own personality, intensifying the work within each person's responsibility, eliminating all the weaknesses such as greed, laziness, and timidity, and developing the advantages of the nation as much as possible. This is the fundamental principle for us to stand in the world. If we can do this, then there will always be a day to settle the accounts for the national crisis and national humiliation. (Xu Zhi's Notes)

Education News

Important News

Ministry of Education's Financial Difficulties

The Ministry of Finance Actually Pays 21,000 Yuan Per Month

The Ministry of Education's funding, according to the original budget of income and expenditure, was 42,000 yuan. Since the national crisis, the Ministry of Finance has reduced it, and the actual monthly payment to the Ministry of Education is 21,000 yuan. Out of this, the Ministry of Education allocates 2,500 yuan per month to the National Institute for Compilation and Translation. In reality, there is a shortfall of only 18,500 yuan, which relies on 25,000 yuan from Zhejiang Province's poppy tax to supplement it. Since the national crisis, only one or two months of poppy tax have been handed over, with significant arrears. It is said that the Ministry of Education is therefore unable to make ends meet and is experiencing extreme financial difficulties.

Record of Minister of Education Wang Shijie Taking Office

Announcing Three Policy Directions

The newly appointed Minister of Education, Wang Shijie, arrived at the Ministry of Education at 8:40 AM on the 8th. First, Vice Minister Duan Xipeng gathered officials of the Ministry of Education above the recommended rank and introduced them to each other in the conference room. Immediately afterwards, he attended the Ministry of Education's memorial week and gave instructions to all members of the Ministry. He first spoke about the future direction of efforts for educational administrative organs, which can be divided into three points: (1) Emphasizing vocational education and seeking the implementation of productive education; (2) Establishing the education budget and planning its security and independence, so that it will not be affected and shaken, and educational undertakings can gradually proceed according to the planned plan; (3) Using educational strength to assist in the popularization of the civil service examination system, selecting true talent and seeking appropriate outlets for young people. Following this, he explained three points to the internal staff: (1) As a principle, old staff will not be changed lightly in order to utilize experienced personnel, hoping they will work with peace of mind; (2) In the future, the promotion of staff will be discussed and a performance evaluation method will be carefully formulated, hoping that they will not request promotion themselves; (3) The work that is in progress and being planned will be discussed in detail with various departments and offices and continued.

After taking office on the 8th, Minister of Education Wang Shijie announced the appointment of Lei　 as Director of the General Affairs Department, Zheng Yanghe as Section Chief of the Second Section of the General Affairs Department, Yu Dehui as Section Chief of the Third Section of the General Affairs Department, and Wang Dehuang as a staff member of the Secretariat.

Ministry of Education Issues Order

Regulations for Filing Scout Training Classes

(Nanjing, 9th) The Ministry of Education has approved the ten articles of the "Regulations for Filing Scout Training Classes" formulated by the Headquarters of the Boy Scouts of China and issued them to all departments and bureaus. From now on, any secondary or higher schools or physical education colleges that establish Scout instructor training classes must follow these regulations.

Local News

Internal Hygiene Department Organizes

Primary and Secondary School Hygiene Picture Competition

Municipal Education Bureau Forwards Order to Schools to Participate

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau yesterday issued an order to the municipal and registered private primary and secondary schools in this city, stating that the Ministry of Education's Instruction No. 3221 stated: "The Internal Affairs Department of Health's official letter stated: 'In order to promote health education and awaken students to develop healthy habits, from the perspective of promoting national health, this Department has specially planned to hold the first phase of the primary and secondary school hygiene picture competition, limited to the four provinces and cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Beijing, and Shanghai. It has sent personnel to consult with your Ministry on handling the matter. Now the competition instructions and other documents have been prepared and printed and are waiting to be distributed. A special letter is sent to your Ministry requesting you to order the education departments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces and the education bureaus of Nanjing and Shanghai to issue instructions to all county education bureaus to forward them to all schools according to the number of existing primary and secondary schools, one instruction sheet and two product certification forms per school, enclosed in envelopes, to be forwarded to all schools for compliance and participation in order to promote its popularization. All schools must follow the provisions in the instructions to prepare for participation in the competition procedures, topics, and drawing sizes. All products from schools must be instructed to be sent by the city and county education bureaus to this Department, with two copies of the competition instructions and registration forms attached. Please investigate and handle this matter and reply accordingly.' The approval is hereby given. Upon investigation, this competition is purely for the purpose of promoting healthy habits and promoting health education. In addition to issuing orders, we hereby issue 370 copies of the instructions for the first phase of the primary and secondary school hygiene picture competition and 740 copies of the product instructions. The Bureau is hereby ordered to instruct all primary and secondary schools under its jurisdiction to participate in this competition and to instruct the art works to be submitted to the Internal Affairs Ministry of Health by the education bureaus of the respective counties and cities within the prescribed time limit. After all matters have been concluded, the handling situation must be reported by the education bureaus of the respective counties and cities to the competent education halls and bureaus for submission to this Ministry for record. Please comply and instruct all subordinates to comply." Upon investigation, the hygiene picture competition is very important in relation to health education. All schools should comply and earnestly organize it and submit it to the Bureau as scheduled for compilation and transfer. We hereby issue one copy of the instructions and 　 copies of the product instructions. Please comply with this order."

Shanghai University's New Five-Year Plan

Since Shanghai University reorganized in the spring of 1928, five years have passed. Thanks to the efforts of the president, faculty, and students, as well as the material and spiritual support from all sectors of society, the atmosphere is vigorous. The five-year plan, such as adding school buildings, expanding library facilities, increasing equipment and specimens, and improving teaching, has been gradually realized and has achieved considerable success. Yesterday, the school held its annual board of directors meeting, attended by board members Li Yaobang, Yu Bingcha, Yu Shouchun, Hu Yongqi, Chen Chunbao, Xu Zhendong, Lin Yuchu, Herbert, and Weiles, and more than ten other people. Important motions, in addition to approving the budget for the next academic year, also stipulated the new five-year plan after this, with a rough outline as follows: (1) Implementing the vocationalization of courses and striving to develop the existing colleges of Arts, Sciences, and Commerce; (2) Limiting enrollment in order to improve teaching effectiveness and pay attention to character training. The university department will have a maximum of 600 students (400 men and 200 women), the business school in the city center will have 600 students, the affiliated middle school will have 400 students, and the Hudong Commune 　night school will have 1,000 students; (3) Improving teaching experiments, the general examination honor program tutorial system, etc.; (4) Improving faculty welfare, savings, pension, etc.; (5) Adding school buildings, auditoriums, classrooms, faculty residences, etc.; (6) Raising more funds and seeking more donations to help out-of-school youth.

Peida Books and Instruments Transported to Zhengzhou

丨A Total of One Hundred and Sixty-Eight Boxes丨Acting President Xu Songming Went to the Station to Take Care of Them丨

(Special Dispatch from Peiping) The first batch of 168 boxes of books and instruments from Peiping University were transported to Zhengzhou by the Pinghan Railway at 3:00 PM today (the 7th), to be stored in the Jincheng Bank. Before the train departed, Lv Jiemin, the director of the general affairs department of the university office, and the heads of the general affairs departments of the seven colleges were all at the station to take care of everything. Acting President Xu Songming made a special inspection. The China Express Transportation Company checked all the wooden boxes one by one, and the train departed on time. The situation of all parties is recorded as follows:

Loading and unloading expenses After the valuable instruments and books of each college were packed, they were originally scheduled to be transported south on the 5th of this month. On the afternoon of the 3rd, the office telephoned each college to inquire about it, and each college requested a postponement. Also, because the iron-clad car had not been allocated, it was decided to transport it to Zhengzhou on the afternoon of the 8th and store it in the Jincheng Bank. The storage fee for each box is 30 cents per month, and the China Express Transportation Company is responsible for the transportation. The loading and unloading fee from Ping to Zheng is six yuan per box. Yesterday, news was received from the transportation sector that a 40-ton iron-clad car had been allocated and started on the 6th to load the car at the West Station, and it would go south on the 7th and arrive in Zhengzhou on the 10th. Because of the nature of the package transportation, there is no need to send an escort.

Number of boxes in each college (1) The Medical College has loaded 44 boxes of instruments from each department, 15 boxes of specimens, and 28 boxes of books, for a total of 87 boxes. (2) The College of Arts has one box of files, one box of registration, one box of books, and one box of instruments, for a total of 5 boxes. (3) The College of Agriculture has 20 boxes of microscopes and specimens from the Department of Biology, 10 boxes of surveying instruments and tree measuring instruments from the Department of Forestry (including one box of wood specimens), 3 boxes of agriculture, 4 boxes of the Department of Economics, and 50 boxes of the library, for a total of 50 boxes. (4) Pingda High School has one box of files. (5) The School of Commerce has one box of documents and one box of books, for a total of 2 boxes. (6) The Pingda Office has two boxes of documents. (7) The School of Law has one box of documents and two boxes of books. (8) The School of Engineering has six boxes of books and twelve boxes of instruments, for a total of 18 boxes. (9) The Women's College of Arts and Sciences may be difficult to transport together because the wooden boxes have not been purchased. The total number of boxes above is 168.

Ministry of Railways Allocates Cars The part of Peiping University's important books and instruments transported to Shanghai has been changed to be stored in Zhengzhou in order to facilitate transportation and save transportation costs. The Ministry of Railways has also approved half-price billing and transportation.

China Swimming Association Builds Pool

The members of the China Swimming Research Association are all responsible for carrying out the problem of building a swimming pool. My Hopes for Our Country's Sports

Liu Xuesong

During my return to China from the United States this time, I witnessed the state of sports in the country and had many feelings. Compared with the advanced European and American countries in sports, we are naturally far behind. However, if we can train seriously and strive to encourage ourselves from now on, we will definitely not fall behind for long. Even in terms of the results of this Shanghai Secondary School Joint Sports Meet, although it is not very outstanding, it has improved slightly compared to before. Yesterday, Dr. Wang Zhengting came to Hangzhou and talked about this matter. He said that in order to improve the overall level of sports and improve results, we should first train talents in middle schools, so that the future can be hopeful. This is a fundamental plan. However, in addition to this, I have to say a word to our sports community, that is, our country's sports have always been only the individual efforts of schools in various places, and it is not very common among the people. Moreover, many students have very good results in school and practice very diligently, but once they graduate, they completely abandon their sports life. How can we seek further progress in this way? Compared with Europe and the United States, these untrained people are naturally far behind. Our country participated in the American Los Angeles World Games for the first time this year. I personally participated in the grand event and witnessed everything. I deeply felt the importance of this move. Although Liu Changchun did not win any points this time, he has made a deep impression on various countries. The American sports community especially has great sympathy for us. People of the country, why not strive to improve ourselves quickly, what will happen later? The 11th Olympic Games in 1936 will be held in Berlin, Germany. I once told representatives from various countries in the United States that China will definitely have excellent performance results next time. If we can train more, select talents, and then we can occupy a place in the world arena. The first thing to work hard now is the National Games on October 10 this year. I sincerely hope that all parts of the country can take this matter seriously, select good talents, and create excellent records. On the one hand, the Far Eastern Games to be held in 匪 in May next year has also sent a letter of invitation. If these selected people are given considerable training, then the shame of the complete defeat in previous years can be slightly avenged. This is my personal hope for our country's sports. However, it is not difficult to say it, but it is difficult to do it. I sincerely hope that the government authorities can promote it and provide strong assistance, so that sports can gradually become widespread. On the one hand, athletes should also be careful to avoid bad habits and cultivate sportsmanship and the spirit of sports. It must be known that an army with discipline is a powerful army, and an athlete who can abide by the rules is able to strive for progress in results. This is really a fundamental principle, so don't ignore it. Last year, the athletes' dormitory at the World Games had a piece of paper hanging on it with three words to encourage them: (1) SPORTSMANSHIP (2) FELLOWSHIP (3) LEADERSHIP. The Zhejiang Provincial Games will be held soon, which can be used to select candidates to participate in the national selection. I also have high hopes for the trip.

Spring and Autumn

Kai County Elder

— Zhan Lu

In the past, there was an old man from Jiang County who, during the Spring and Autumn period, merely said a few humorous words, expressing his age as a mixed-number of Jiazi (sexagenary cycle). The Jin officials' mathematical knowledge was too rudimentary at the time, and they did not dare use such things as division to solve the problem. As a result, they were startled and made a fuss for a while, and that seventy-three-year-old man from Jiang County has been passed down from two thousand several hundred years ago to this day. No wonder Bernard Shaw loved to tell jokes; it turns out that telling jokes has such a great effect.

The death of Li Qingyun, an old man from Kai County, has been reported in the Chongqing dispatch in the newspapers, stating that he was two hundred and fifty-six years old when he finally left the mortal world. The "Qing" character in Qingyun's name is probably a misspelling of the "Qing" character (庆). I remember that in the 17th year of the Republic of China, newspapers in Shanghai widely published a photograph of an elderly man from Sichuan named Li Qingyun, stating that he was two hundred and fifty years old and was from Shanchuan Village in Kai County. Although his age was high, his spirit in the photograph was very clear and vigorous. Unexpectedly, in just five or six years, he still could not escape this gate of life and death; he succumbed to the god of death after all.

The old man from Kai County has passed away. His age exceeded the old man from Jiang County by three times plus thirty-seven seventy-thirds. If the higher the age, the further the transmission, then the old man from Jiang County has been transmitted for two thousand several hundred years, and the old man from Kai County should be famous for seven or eight thousand years. However, I don't think so! The wheel of time keeps turning. The four characters "Old Man from Jiang County" will never fade away, but I am afraid that the name of the old man from Kai County will not be deeply imprinted in people's minds.

Being able to say a few humorous words, being able to express one's age as a mixed-number of Jiazi, being able to make the Jin officials startled and amazed, this is the old man from Jiang County's ability to be passed down. I wonder if the old man from Kai County had such an ability? If not, then after many years, everyone will only know the old man from Jiang County, and no one will know the old man from Kai County.

For a person to strive for immortality, age is not the most important thing; just look at Yan Hui of Confucius' school and Zhou Yu of the Three Kingdoms period.

Selling Children

— Xiao Xianxian

"Selling children," is one of the emerging slogans that shroud Shanghai in economic recession, and it has the same effect as "clearance sales regardless of cost, buy one get one free" in attracting customers. If you don't believe me, look, on the streets and in the alleys, in front of stores equipped with a wireless telephone or employing a band of foreign musicians, there are always many distinguished guests who stand around with their hands behind their backs, "looking" but not "patronizing." On the streets and in the alleys, there is a carrying pole for "selling children" parked, and likewise, there are always many distinguished guests who stand around with their hands behind their backs, "looking" but not "patronizing."

Indeed, recently, more and more people have been coming to Shanghai from Henan and Shaanxi to "sell children," so that Shanghai's "children" have become in a surplus situation, "stomach sluggish." But to solve this problem, which is neither too big nor too small, in this early twenty-first century when all countries feel overpopulation, I am afraid it cannot be as "stable, fast, and convenient" as when the Imperial Army occupied the Shenyang Arsenal.

Whether "selling children" is a tragic scene is a matter of opinion. In this "iron-blood save the country" era, I believe that the internal organs in the human body should all be steel-ified and transformed into "hard intestines." When people's snot and tears are stuck together as they sell children, I only think of it as a big sale due to the recession, because occasionally there is a "reactionary philanthropist" who separates people's flesh and blood and buys a child with silver dollars. In this civilized world where no one cares about "human meat buns," they are unlikely to make meat filling out of the children. At most, they will just make the children slaves for a lifetime. In this era when anyone can hope to be a slave, what is so pitiful about being a slave?

"It is a small matter to starve to death, but a great matter to lose one's chastity." No one pities prostitutes who sell their chastity or traitors who sell their conscience, but everyone is alarmed when refugees sell their children to avoid starvation. This is indeed a mystery that can be understood but cannot be understood.

Man or Woman?

— Ren Ying

This kind of trick has happened to me for the second time.

The first time, I took a bus on Mystery Street before it was destroyed. I was heading towards Hongkou Park, thinking of breathing in some fresh air to relieve the suffocation accumulated in the city.

The bus was packed with people, and the passengers all focused their eyes on a strangely handsome young man in a Western suit sitting in the right corner. He was holding a bouquet of flowers in his hand, and next to him sat a companion — a strangely beautiful woman.

Following the gaze of the crowd, I also cast my eyes on them, and couldn't help but laugh out loud. Wasn't this strangely handsome young man actually a beautiful girl dressed as a man? The wheels of the bus kept moving forward, and many people were paying attention to this "fake husband." Her demeanor was so natural, not containing any trace of shyness!

Hongkou Park arrived, and we followed a crowd of people, including the fake husband, into the gate of the park.

Again, I stepped onto Old Target Road, which was being destroyed along with Greater Shanghai, to visit one of my classmates — a famous writer. After the classmate's repeated invitations, I went to a luxurious restaurant with some artistic atmosphere. At a round table covered with a silk tablecloth, we were drinking and chatting lightly, placing my insignificant self in the palace of art. When the glass door opened, two fashionable young people came in. My friend greeted the taller one and, at the same time, with a surprised look, greeted the shorter one with a delicate face, saying:

"Miss Xu, I almost didn't recognize you today."

So we exchanged business cards at the same table.

Long Novel

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Six: Sweet and Bitter Love Field, Coldly Observing Two Faces, Rugged Worldly Path, Secret Agreement for Three Years

At this time, the lady was all smiles, seemingly forgetting about the demonstration she had just participated in, shouting "Down with Japanese Imperialism!" Moreover, she was as gentle as water, not like someone with such passionate and heroic spirit. Looking at it, how sweet, does life in this world, not need a member of the opposite sex, to comfort you for a while? Short story

Conscription (Part 1)

— Tian Hensen

It was a tranquil village. Although the country was in crisis, many houses had been reduced to ashes under airplane bombs, and many heads had been separated from their bodies under guns and bayonets; this village was still very tranquil. Only a few people who occasionally went to the city faintly heard talk of fighting, but they didn't quite understand who was fighting whom. At that time, they couldn't help but be instinctively surprised, eager to ask acquaintances where the fighting was taking place and how far it was from here. And after hearing that the fighting was taking place far from here, they were relieved and didn't bother to investigate who was fighting whom. When they returned to the village, they naturally talked about it with the villagers, but everyone was the same, only asking how far away it was, and then not talking much about it. Everyone didn't feel any fear or interest in it.

It was even more tranquil at night. Because it was dark, everyone had already eaten dinner and was preparing to go to bed. When eating dinner, they often ate while watching the sun set in the west, so very few people lit lamps and went to bed. The nights were even more tranquil, with only the sound of dogs barking occasionally, as tranquil as if the city had declared martial law in the middle of the night.

Suddenly, a thunderbolt shattered the tranquility of the village, causing instant chaos. Many families were crying, and only the families of old women Li and fathers San who had no sons, and old men Yang and fathers Zhang who only had daughters, were somewhat quieter. At first, they were equally shocked by the thunderbolt, equally startled, as if it was the end of the world; later, they heard that it was conscription, and then they understood. Those without sons or with only daughters were completely exempt from this suffering. However, the son-in-law of old man Yang was on the list to be conscripted; his daughter suddenly cried and came back; old man Yang realized and became anxious again!

Old man Yang's daughter's childhood name was Little Dog. She was used to being called by her childhood name, and even when she grew up, she was still called Dog Girl. Because she was the only daughter, and her mother died when she was five years old, she was very spoiled, and he was reluctant to marry her off, planning to recruit a son-in-law. But he didn't agree to those who were too good, and old man Yang didn't want to recruit those who were too bad. Those who were good weren't willing to be Yang's son-in-law, so Dog Girl was left until she was twenty-five years old. Her widowed aunt and paternal aunt both advocated that she couldn't be delayed any longer, and persuaded her father to change his mind, that he didn't necessarily have to recruit a son-in-law. Only then did they rely on a matchmaker to arrange for her to marry Little Bull, the second son of Liu Sanye in the same village, resulting in a marriage between a bull and a dog.

The son-in-law, Little Bull, happened to be the same age as Dog Girl, and his appearance wasn't bad. He just had a few pockmarks on his face, but they weren't too unsightly. Dog Girl had only been married for three months and was quite satisfied, and she hadn't said anything bad about him in front of her father. But old man Yang was always worried that Liu Sanye had three sons. Now there were only two daughters-in-law. When the fourteen-year-old youngest son also got married, it would inevitably be a bit difficult to be a daughter-in-law.

However, Dog Girl wasn't worried about these things, because her eldest sister-in-law was a very good person. She was currently enjoying the sweet wine of her new marriage, unexpectedly encountering conscription, forcing her husband to leave her to go to the battlefield. This thunderbolt almost shook her soul out of her body. After crying for a while at home, there was nothing she could do, so she cried to her father.

"Why are you crying like this? Speak properly!" Old man Yang frowned and asked.

"Dad, don't you know? Little Bull is being forced to go to war, and he's leaving tomorrow, Dad! What's going on?" Dog Girl's crying stopped for a moment when she spoke, and she cried again when she said the last sentence.

"Oh! Little Bull was conscripted! I had already expected it just now, Little Bull has three brothers, one of them will have to be conscripted. What is Little Bull doing now?"

"Little Bull doesn't want to go, but the committee in the city won't agree, and he can't help himself. Dad! Do you have any good ideas?" Dog Girl stopped crying again and looked up at old man Yang. Her two eyes, soaked in tears, were full of hope and a pleading look.

Page 13

Free Talk

From Sheng Xuanhuai to Justified Oppression

— Ding Meng

The Sheng family's ancestors accumulated a lot of virtue, so their descendants held two grand ceremonies to "recover lost territory": one was under Yuan Shikai's Republic of China government, and the other is under the current National Government.

In the early years of the Republic, Sheng Xuanhuai was said to be the number one traitor, and his family property was confiscated. Soon, it seems after the Second Revolution, it was returned. That was not strange, because Yuan Shikai was "hurt by the same kind," he himself was also a traitor. Aren't we commemorating May Seventh and May Ninth every year? Yuan Shikai signed the Twenty-One Demands, there is real evidence of his betrayal.

Recently, I found this piece of news in the newspaper, roughly saying: "The Sheng family's property has long been ordered to be returned, such as the Lingering Garden in Suzhou, and the pawnshops in Jiangyin and Wuxi, etc., are currently being processed for return." This really surprised me. After inquiring, I heard that when the National Revolutionary Army first arrived in Huning in the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, Sheng's family property was confiscated again; the crime this time was probably "local tyrant and evil gentry." Gentry is even to "evil," plus the old crime of betrayal, naturally it should be confiscated again. But why is it being returned again?

First, we should not suspect that there are traitors now, because there is no real evidence — people now have long sworn not to sign treaties that humiliate the country, they are not like Sheng Xuanhuai and Yuan Shikai. Second, we are currently raising funds for air donations, which shows that the government's finances are not well-off. So, why?

The result of academic research is that oppression originally has two kinds: one is justified and will always be justified, and the other is unjustified. The justified ones are like forcing the common people to repay high-interest loans and pay land rent; the "reason" for this kind of oppression is written on the notice: "Borrowing money and repaying debts is a principle common to China and foreign countries, renting land and paying taxes is an unchanging rule since ancient times." The unjustified ones are the confiscation of Sheng Xuanhuai's family property, etc.; this method of "oppressing" great gentry may have been justified locally, but it has long become unjustified now.

When I first saw the "Letter to Workers" on May 1st published in the newspaper, saying: "Resist the unjustified oppression of domestic capitalists," I was also surprised. Isn't this advocating class struggle? Later, I thought about it and understood. This is saying that unjustified oppression should be opposed, while justified oppression is not included. As for how it is justified, you will understand when you read on, the following says: "Must be hardworking and endure hardship, step up production... Should especially share the difficulties together, strive for genuine cooperation between labor and capital, and eliminate all disputes between labor and capital." There is also saying that "Chinese workers are not as miserable as foreign workers" and so on. I thought to myself, fortunately I didn't shout out in alarm, things in the world are always reasonable, and so is all oppression. Moreover, although there are very few reasons for dealing with Sheng Xuanhuai and others, there will always be reasons for dealing with workers.

Untitled

— Zhao Tianren

Recently, as soon as I see a pen, infinite annoyance and infinite anger immediately rise from my heart. It's as if a wild beast that has been shot by a hunter once and occasionally sees the hunter's incomplete rifle again, when I see a pen, I want to run away, I harbor hostility.

This, I understand myself, my hatred for the pen is not without reason. Indeed, in recent years, the wounds and torments that the pen has given me have really been unbearable.

Friends in my hometown often write letters asking me what exactly I do in Shanghai. Sometimes I humbly say: "I make a living by 'penning' in Shanghai," and sometimes I arrogantly and arrogantly reply: "I am doing cultural movement in Shanghai!" Only God knows what I do in Shanghai.

Life is as dull as a mechanical operation, every morning, in addition to washing my face and brushing my teeth, the first thing I do is to find my pen. I hold my pen, tightly, my eyes, my attention, even my whole body's energy, are concentrated on the tip of the pen, and my brain juice seeps out drop by drop from the tip of the pen. At this time, I have no pain, even no feeling. Because I am just a machine, squeezing out brain juice is not a job, but just an obligation.

Sometimes, when the night is quiet and the moon is bright, I temporarily put down my pen, as if releasing a heavy burden from my shoulders, and drag my heavy feet on the street that sleeps like a dead snake, rushing towards my home. The moon shines overhead, the shadow drags behind me, and the sound of my own footsteps awakens me from a day's fatigue, "What is it all for?" I ask myself, looking at the cold moon, looking at the stars that are winking at people, I often only let out a soft bitter laugh.

Taking a machine as my metaphor, I think, this is the most appropriate. Isn't a machine soulless? Doesn't it only operate naturally according to certain rules? What about me? People say that I am a free person with a soul, and I myself don't seem to feel that I am not a free person with a soul. But, when I pick up a pen, questions immediately arise in my mind, am I a free person with a soul? I can't help but say what I don't want to say, and I can't say what I want to say. My will, my thoughts, my freedom, are all imprisoned at this time. I am just a loudspeaker, an echo, even a mobile typewriter. I remember Bernard Shaw once said, "In capitalist society, everyone auctions themselves off, women auction their bodies, and men auction their souls." Whenever the night is late and quiet, I think back to the day's events, and I vaguely hear my auctioned soul crying and complaining to me, and I vaguely see several masks on my face, so I scratch my face with all my strength, I am ashamed, I regret, and finally I cry bitterly.

For the sake of life, I auctioned off my soul, for the sake of life, I auctioned off my youth. I eat my own brain juice, chew my own soul, is it bitter? Is it astringent? Only I myself know. God, is this life? Thus, every time I see a pen, I harbor hostility, I want to run away, but until now I still have to find my pen every day, hold it, tightly. I think, one day I will have to put down this crap, one day I will have to call back my soul.

Dantian

— Cao Juren

Below the navel, there is a wonderful place, technically called "Dantian" "Dantian" is a unique and precious place. Baopuzi says: Midnight and midday are the times when heaven and earth generate energy; sit cross-legged facing east, deeply inhale into the body, slowly send it into the Dantian, and then slowly exhale. When learning, guide the breath into the nose, practice breath counting, counting one, two, three, four, up to one hundred and twenty times, then slowly exhale it. Because the amount of air inhaled must be finer than the amount of air exhaled, so specially place a feather on the nose to check whether it moves. Apply this breath counting to walking, and if you can ensure the air is inhaled, then you will begin to have some effect. Ji Shuye said: "Breathe and exhale, nourish the body; body and spirit are close, inside and out are complete. Inaction is self-attainment, body is subtle and mind is profound; you can compare longevity with Xianmen, compete years with Wang Qiao." This secret of cultivation, practiced for a long time, has infinite wonderful uses!

Below the "Dantian", there are also wonderful places, which are said to be related to health preservation; how to preserve health? See the art of the bedroom, and you still have to ask Mr. Ye Dehui, but unfortunately he is already dead. According to the news in Shanghai newspapers, such as the old painter in Suzhou sucking a virgin's something something, and a certain boss in Shanghai eating a virgin boy's something something, the reporters' vivid descriptions are like they had seen it with their own eyes; then in addition to the art of the bedroom, there is also this method of collecting and replenishing that goes hand in hand with exhalation and guidance. To exhale, to bedroom, to collect and replenish, all are nothing more than wanting to become immortal, as for the pale and thin faces of the virgin boys and girls, that is not in question.

Those who cultivate also say that speaking should not exceed the throat gate; too much talk damages energy, speaking from the chest or abdomen will greatly deplete vital energy, this secret of health preservation is exactly the opposite of the breathing method, one seeks depth, one seeks shallow output, each obtaining wonderful use. Also, sadness and anger are enough to shake the spirit; those who have attained enlightenment always have a smiling face, with Maitreya Buddha as proof. Speaking of it, in the end, the main point is to cultivate the "Dantian".

The ancients said: "If one son attains enlightenment, even chickens and dogs become immortals," the "Dantian" must be guided, collected, and replenished to cultivate it. Some say: "I often travel between Beijing, Shanghai, Tianjin, Guangdong, Fujian, Hunan, and Hubei, and I have met many who have 'smiling faces and speak in the mouth', why?" It is said: "These are all enlightened people — although no one sees the cultivation and synthesis, heaven knows the intention! These are all enlightened people!"

Carrot Top's Whiskers

— by Jules Renard, translated by Lin Qu

Bathing (Continued)

"Yes," said Carrot Top's Whiskers, "though I don't particularly enjoy doing this. Water gets in my ears, and I'll get a headache."

He looked for a place to learn to swim, which meant finding a place where he could move his arms while keeping his knees on the sand as he moved forward.

"You're too impatient," said Lepic to him. "Don't thrash around like you're pulling your hair, clenching your fists and making a fuss. You should also move those legs of yours that you're not using."

"Swimming without using your legs is even harder," said Carrot Top's Whiskers.

But his older brother Felix constantly disturbed him, preventing him from focusing. "Carrot Top's Whiskers, come here. It's deeper here. My feet can't touch the bottom, I'm sinking. Look. Hey: you can still see me now. Be careful: now you can't see me. Now, you stand over by the willow tree. Don't move. I bet I can get to you in just six strokes."

"I'll count for you," said Carrot Top's Whiskers, shivering. His shoulders were above the water, motionless like a real boundary marker. He squatted back down in the water, ready to swim. But Felix climbed on his back, somersaulted into the water, and said to him: "Now it's your turn. You can climb on my back if you want."

"Let me just learn to swim in peace," said Carrot Top's Whiskers.

"Alright," shouted Lepic, "come out, come here and have some sugared wine."

"We're going to have wine!" said Carrot Top's Whiskers.

Now he simply didn't want to come out. He hadn't had enough swimming. The river, which he was now about to leave, no longer frightened him. Just now it had been as heavy as lead, but now it was as light as a feather. He bravely struggled in the water, risking danger, as if he were prepared to sacrifice his life to save someone, and he even willingly submerged himself in the water to experience the torment of those who drown themselves.

"Come on quickly," shouted Lepic, "or your older brother Felix will drink all the sugared wine."

Although Carrot Top's Whiskers didn't particularly like sugared wine, he said:

"I'll never let anyone take my share."

He drank the wine like a battle-hardened soldier.

Lepic: Your bath isn't clean enough. There's still dirt on your ankles.

Carrot Top's Whiskers: It's mud, Papa.

Lepic: No, it's dirt.

Carrot Top's Whiskers: Then should I go back and wash again, Papa?

Lepic: We'll wash tomorrow. We'll come again.

Carrot Top's Whiskers: That depends on luck! We'll only come again if the weather is good!

He dabbed at his body with the dry corner of the towel that Felix had wet. His head was heavy, and his throat was bitter, and he laughed heartily when his brother and Lepic made amusing jokes about his shriveled toes. (Correction) Yesterday, in the twenty-eighth line of "Carrot Top's Whiskers," "apple seed" was a misprint for "apple candy."

Su and Zhejiang Spring Silkworm Season Approaching

(Nanjing) In each previous silkworm season, the Silkworm Improvement Association distributed improved varieties, and graduates from the Silkworm Department of Jinling University went to various silkworm areas to guide breeding, with better results. This year, the rural economy is in a state of panic, and the mulberry trees are producing leaves later. Farmers are very indifferent to silkworm affairs. Although there is breeding in various townships and Xiaodanyang near the city, the number of silkworm eggs is reduced. The weather is sunny and warm, and the improved varieties being bred are developing smoothly. The students are still going to various townships as usual to guide the progress. The early batch has already reached the stage of big sleep and abundant leaves, and the late batch is still in the third sleep and opening leaves.

(Chang'an) The earliest place is near Xucun and other places. Although most of the native silkworms being bred were abandoned due to the bad weather, the remaining healthy silkworm eggs are developing well due to the sunny and warm weather and have large eyes and abundant leaves, and there are occasionally small clusters of cocoons being made. However, the improved silkworms being re-bred have undergone good development and are healthy after the first sleep. The early batch will also enter the fourth sleep and start spinning, and the late batch will have the third sleep and opening leaves in three or four days, and new cocoons will soon be available on the market.

Only 30% of the usual number

Some silk merchants contracted to purchase
