Page 15

Talk

Sometimes

— Lin Huiyin

"Forgive me, God, please take back all my heat, all my light," the sun pleaded wistfully.

Since being created, who knows how many years have passed, the sun has always stood there, motionless. However, what he finds annoying is not just his own motionless standing, but also the Earth's ceaseless rotation; because, if there were no rotation, perhaps he wouldn't feel the pointlessness of his standing. Moreover, the Earth rotates so monotonously, so unchangingly. If he himself could rotate, he believed he could rotate in some different ways. Sometimes he got so angry that he wouldn't look at the Earth, closing his eyes tightly. But as soon as he opened his eyes, he saw the Earth again, and saw the Earth's rotation.

"Oh, tirelessly rotating Earth, you actually rotate so tirelessly!"

Sometimes, he was angry with himself, condemning himself: "You stupid thing, can you only be so fixed?" So he used all his strength, only wanting to spin once. But there was no effect.

"What's the point of living like this?" He began to doubt life. "If I can only live like this, I'd rather not live," he made his final decision.

But he still stood there rigidly, only emitting heat, only emitting light. Finally, he saw that there was no hope for himself, so he shouted out the plea to destroy his own life:

"Forgive me, God, please take back all my heat, all my light."

Saving the Nation and Saving Hearts

— Ding Hua

Since the Japanese invaded and occupied the Eastern Provinces, due to the many patriotic compatriots, the methods of saving the nation that have been widely spread in society have also emerged endlessly and have been new every day. What with saving the nation through recreational performances, saving the nation through donations, it is really too much to write about and too much to remember. A says: If China wants to resist Japan, it must first develop the resources of the country, so that the economy is not worried about lack, and can safely resist the enemy without any worries. B advocates that if China wants to resist foreign aggression, it must first expand its military force. C says that purchasing a large number of aircraft and training aviation talents is the only shortcut to resisting aggression. Some people are also proposing to reorganize the Chinese navy. Everyone has their own views and issues their own brilliant theories. But can this handful of national salvation policies really save China?

Let us think carefully. If the development of China's resources becomes a reality, and China is indeed very rich, but who knows if these people in power and those who control the government will no longer be solely profit-oriented, fighting for power and gain with each other, and be able to use the abundance of the economy to engage in resistance against aggression and recuperation? I'm afraid the result will only be to increase the large amounts of deposits that the important people put in foreign banks, and issue a few more exorbitant taxes. As for expanding the military, even if one day, China's army, navy, and air force become elite troops, and all kinds of firearms are manufactured to be very sophisticated, who dares to guarantee that these people who hold military power will unanimously point their guns outwards and no longer fight among themselves? I'm afraid that once they start fighting again, because of the sophistication of the firearms and the strength of the soldiers, the suffering of our ordinary people will be several times worse than before and now; in this way, national affairs will be in even worse shape, so how can we talk about resisting aggression and saving the nation?

Therefore, in the current China, what it urgently needs is still "saving hearts"! Why did Zhang Xueliang not resist? Why did Tang Yulin abandon Rehe and flee? Why was Hu Lifu willing to be a traitor? Why was Puyi willing to be a Japanese puppet? Why did the people inside the Guan watch the suffering of their compatriots outside the Guan without offering help? All these things are because the hearts of those involved have problems, or have undergone abnormal changes, so to resist aggression and save the nation, we must start with saving hearts!

What is meant by saving hearts is, in a small sense, to transform a lazy heart into a diligent one, a non-resistant heart into a resistant one, a heart that only cares about personal gain into a heart that only cares about public gain, and a heart that is brave in internal warfare into one that is brave in resisting aggression. In a larger sense, transform four hundred million different hearts into one. When that time comes, everyone will be willing to do things based on their conscience, internal wars will be eliminated, and all industries will prosper. Using this to resist aggression, what aggression cannot be eliminated? Using this to attack the enemy, what enemy cannot be destroyed?

"There is no greater sorrow than the death of the heart." In the current China, the work of saving hearts is at least more urgent, necessary, and effective than other national salvation policies!

Literary Arts

May

— Yan

May has a scant thirty-one days, painful commemorations occupy seven, treat approaching enemies like formidable foes and defend against laborers like soldiers, beside the Lu kingdom city is a miserable white cold, on Nanjing Road is a fresh red overflow, Don't mention the heartbreaking May 7th and 9th, in one month there are three times of kneeling down. Wireless

The scene vaguely resembles peace and prosperity, every household broadcasts music, enjoy today's pleasure today, don't wait until the country is lost for the song to be unfinished.

Pessimism and Optimism

— Jin Zhi

In times of chaos, pessimistic thoughts are most likely to occur and spread. As soon as we sense some kind of social or personal unease, we will cry out, "Life is too meaningless!" In reality, we are all a bunch of numb people, otherwise, in this kind of unfair environment, what wouldn't make us heartbroken? We seem to be traveling in a graveyard full of dead bodies, what we see and hear is either tragic or miserable. Tragic scenes cannot be described by pen and ink. Everything around is narrow, selfish, and a despicable illusion. People no longer believe in ideals; immediate benefits seem to be the ideals and motives of most people. The question of right and wrong is not a question; the question is whether it is beneficial or not. If it is beneficial, I will do it; if it is not beneficial, no matter how noble the ideal or cause, I will never approve of it. This is the inner thought of those who call themselves progressive people recently. How can this situation not make people pessimistic? No wonder a floating, romantic life has become a fashionable life. "Floating! I am now like duckweed in the sea, floating with the wind, not knowing where the other shore is?" So-called new poets often have these kinds of similar sentences. "I hate life! I would rather go to a deserted place and live a pure and free life. Life is too ugly, where is my beautiful paradise? I want to seek my paradise! I want to be separated from this evil world!! Never see humans, who look like animals but are not animals and are called 'the spirit of all things'!" When we write articles, we can write these sentences, and we will definitely get the sympathy of the public. Yes, everyone is bathing in the sea, and烦恼 is a modern-day epidemic. People want to get rid of烦恼, so they often send out those cries. Everyone wants to be happy, everyone doesn't want to struggle in pain, but pain often accompanies them, choking their throats every step of the way. No wonder they are running on the road of pessimism!

In the eyes of pessimists, everyone is evil, and human society cannot be transformed. They often laugh at social idealists for meddling, and often regard revolutionaries as madmen. "Life is a painful natural history," "Survival is evil," the world's philosophers tell us. But since we are born into the world, can we just curse life like this? Can we just hate people like this? Do we have no way to seek an elixir to reduce pain in pain? What is the use of pessimism! Let's move forward as soon as possible! Pessimists, please put down your depressed hearts and strive to move straight on the road to improving life! Sighing long and hiding in the mountains and forests is ultimately useless.

The privileged people of the present world are used to living in one-sided happiness, often wearing red-colored glasses, thinking that life is most blessed. Pain? Sorrow? Although they sometimes have pain and sorrow due to family discord and the failure of speculative businesses, they usually think that social reformers are making a fuss about nothing when they speak out for the poor. In their minds, everyone in the world seems to be as happy and happy as they are. Destroying their comfort is a rebellious act! This is what the saying goes, "When you are full, you don't know that others are hungry!" Beautiful women! Fine wine! Luxury cars! Angry horses! They have everything, how can they say that life is painful?

These people are ignorant and unfeeling pig-like optimists! They are extremely optimistic about life. Because they are deaf, they cannot hear the cries of the miserable world.

But, some other people have a special thought, thinking that everything in humanity is good, and even the most evil things, in their view, are also an expression of goodness. Although they are not privileged, they do not hate life either. They see all phenomena as gifts from nature. We should not think too much or worry too much. We just need to live by fate. Whether the result is good or bad, we don't need to meddle. Good things will be good, and bad things, you can worry to death and it will be useless: so it is better to implement the idea of "enjoy today's wine today, and worry about tomorrow's money tomorrow," which is much more thorough. There are also countless of these people in today's society. We cannot name them, but we call them muddleheaded, inexplicable optimists.

These people are also enemies of revolution. They feel that revolution will disturb their clear dreams of enjoyment, and it is better to live in a drunken乡. If the future of mankind is good, then naturally we don't need to make any serious efforts, and it will be good. So let's just be sloppy! They take sloppiness as their slogan, and everything can be done with the four characters of sloppiness. Pity! Advocates of sloppiness!

Can life be optimistic? Where can we be optimistic? We only need to look at the current phenomenon, and we will be full of sorrow.

Pessimistic? Optimistic? If we carefully examine humanity, we feel that pessimism and optimism are really not needed in humanity. People have good and evil, construction and destruction, noble and despicable. In short, the road of evolution needs people to explore.

Prison Life

— Yan Zhao

Several old-fashioned Chinese houses, with clumsy wooden fences arranged under the eaves, the light in the room is not very sufficient; not only is it not sufficient, it is simply dark. The people in the room are lying all over the place, even the corners are crowded. They are all very haggard, their hair is as fluffy as autumn weeds, and their skin is as yellow and thin as fallen leaves; their faces seem to be about to burst into tears, and the state of weariness, depression, worry, and indignation is self-evident. Their bodies seem to be weak, and their hands and feet are also very weak; some of them also have heavy iron chains tied to their ankles, so they can't walk at all. These are probably people with heavier sins.

The entire room is filled with evil atmosphere, which may be the reason why people living in prison life have no vitality. Here, the cage is so small, the place is so dirty, the people are so crowded, and life is so unfree, how can it not evolve into decadence and depression, to the point of closing one's eyes and dying?

Their food and drink cannot be said to be delicacies from mountains and seas; even vegetarian dishes are difficult to fill your stomach. What's even worse is at night, when they should be able to sleep for a while to nourish their overly tired and exhausted bodies and spirits, but the lice, as numerous as hairs, come to bother them! The old 百虱 doesn't care about your life or death, clamps onto you with one bite, and doesn't let go until death, trying its best to eat and suck your precious blood, sucking until it is full and then quietly hiding in the seams of your clothes; the jumping flea敏捷ly uses its innate jumping ability, jumps into the chest of the big guy, then jumps into the arm of the young man, and then jumps to the leg of the old man, jumping back and forth, jumping all over the cage, sucking all the blood from everyone's body; the cunning bedbug is even more恶人, even more sneaky and辣泼, every time when the night is deep and people are quiet, it secretly drills out from the floor seams to disturb their dreams and牛drink their朱殷. They can't bear it anymore, they jump up forcefully, crying sadly. And no one will pity them, still剥削ing the bloody blood from their bodies and muscles.

Outside the fence stood a majestic and awe-inspiring prison guard, with piercing eyes, watching the inside of the fence. He doesn't allow you to speak, and even less does he allow you to move. If you accidentally say a word, he will immediately叱然吆喝, scaring you out of your wits. If a few people with more courage still want to say a few more words, he will send you a heavy and painful beating with a big stick.

They have no years, no months, no mornings, no evenings, imprisoned in this prison, unable to see the blue sky, unable to see the sun and moon, dimly,阴霾霾, passing the confusing 光阴. Freedom of speech is not allowed, and thoughts have no freedom, and actions are even less free, as if sitting in a檻穽, enduring that restrained life. 丨丨Life is difficult, and death is impossible.

It is said that the prison here is our noble country, and the people in the prison must be the compatriots of our noble country; the life in the prison is naturally the life of our compatriots.

Ah! Compatriots... prison... life...

(In support of donations to righteous troops)

When is a person considered old?

— Pei

When is a person considered old?

Sir Walter Scott, at the age of fifty-five, lamented that he had become an old man. The French writer Montaigne retired to his villa at the age of thirty and lived his quiet reading life. The British writer Dr. Samuel Johnson said: A person reaches the peak of his life at the age of thirty-five, and then he has to walk downhill. According to physiology, a person can live to be one hundred to one hundred and fifty years old, so why are people like Scott so young and considered old? The answer is: because they feel old, so their behavior is old. Physiologist William James (WITL J S) said, "Most people become outdated old pines by the age of twenty-five." This statement really grasped the truth. People at the age of twenty-five are mostly satisfied with their careers; they already have "prejudice", which is the so-called "doctrine", and reject all new ideas; they have stopped "growing".

As long as a person stops growing, no matter how old he is, he begins to "age". On the other hand, truly great people are never old. The Italian painter Titian lived to be ninety-nine years old and never stopped painting. Goethe died at the age of eighty-three, completing the great "Faust" a few years before his death. Gladstone was seventy years old when he had to learn a foreign language. The great French mathematician Laplace died at the age of seventy-eight, still working. He shouted before his death: "What we know is nothing, what we don't know is much more!" When is a person considered old? Then you get the real answer. Laplace was still not satisfied when he was seventy, and he was convinced that there was infinite knowledge in the world; he was still "growing"; he was still a young man! A person who can maintain this attitude, and can say "I have grown!" when looking back on the past every year, is a young man. The day he no longer grows, he says to himself, "I have completely acquired the knowledge I need."丨His youth is nearing extinction. No matter whether he is twenty-five years old or seventy-five years old, there is no difference, from that day on, he is considered truly old.

Clerk Correspondence

Dragging People Down

Editor Mr.:

Before I ask you to solve my difficulties, let me first talk about my family situation. I have an old mother, two younger brothers, and two younger sisters. I am the eldest, and I am forty-four years old this year; my father was sacrificed in the "January 28th" battle last year. When he was alive, his monthly salary was more than three hundred yuan; therefore, the family's expenses and the tuition fees of my younger siblings were not a problem. After his death, I! Unfortunate eldest child! I have to take on this heavy burden alone. Although I am a high school graduate, I am currently a small clerk in a company with a monthly salary of thirty yuan. Isn't there a big difference between thirty yuan and three hundred yuan? It is already very difficult to use it to support the family's daily expenses, let alone provide for my younger brother's tuition fees (one in the second year of high school and one still in elementary school), it is really difficult. According to my mother's idea, she wanted to ask my eldest brother to go to work; but I think a person must at least have received a high school education to have common knowledge to stand in society, so I still strongly advocate that he continue to study, although my strength is very weak.

Now let me talk about my difficulties. My colleagues in the company are all playboys, either eating花酒 or gambling. Once, they asked me to join, but I refused. Therefore, they hold a grudge in their hearts and look for my faults everywhere to report to the manager; their intention is a kind of warning, and they are not allowed to refuse any of their orders. Alas! According to their behavior, logically I should advise him as a friend, and if he doesn't listen, I should report it to the manager. Now I am a weak person, and in order to protect this饭碗 that my family of six relies on to live on, I have already taken a policy of non-resistance. They seem to be satisfied; why do they have to drag people down? If this continues, sooner or later my position will be insecure. Thinking of this, it really makes people feel chills; sir, can you point out a bright road and give me some fighting power? I wish you

Good health Shao Fei respectfully

X X X

Editor's Note: For Shao Jun's family, it is indeed very difficult to maintain household expenses with thirty yuan a month. As for a person standing in society, knowledge is of course essential. Your brother is already in the second year of high school, and in another year, he will graduate from high school and come to an end. You are right to advocate that he continue to study until he graduates from high school. As for the tuition fees, it is best if you can raise them; otherwise, you may as well borrow money to achieve it. Borrowing money out of necessity for legitimate tuition fees, people will probably not refuse; for you, this debt, in the future, you may as well ask your brother to share the responsibility of repayment. You should also let your brother know about your painstaking planning; this is not necessarily a basis for him to repay the debt in the future, but at the same time, it is also good to let him know the difficulty of material resources and work hard.

As for the problem between you and your colleagues, we advise you not to worry too much. The reason why they must drag people down is nothing more than a guilty conscience, fearing that you will not only not fool around, but also say their faults. Since you have already embraced the policy of non-resistance, after a long time, knowing your thoughts, they will be able to live in peace. You only need to work hard and avoid mistakes as much as possible. On the side of the employer, even if he does not have the courage to eliminate the playboys, or he himself is a playboy, he will not absolutely be unable to tolerate you!

Finally, we also want to make a minimum demand on Shao Jun's colleagues and other playboys in other places: "Even if you cannot restrain yourself and love yourself, at least don't drag down those who restrain themselves: you must know that even if you let them go, is it harmful to you?"

Fiction

The Life of the Five Beauties (5) (Continued)

— Ling He

Five First Time for Gu

No matter how the world mocks them, Miss Liu finally grew up. To her, these long years seemed like a dream. She didn't even know how she grew up. Maybe she deliberately wanted to forget as much as possible, because she often said: "What is this, isn't it just this way?" Then, the corners of her mouth turned down, and she snorted a bitter laugh from her nose. In the eyes of sentimental people, this is very touching and can make them shed tears for her, but over time, it is no longer strange, and it seems that people are bound to do so. In fact, our Miss Liu is not very willing to understand herself. For example, there are often many嫖客搂着 her waist and praising her sadly:

"My little baby, you don't know how beautiful you are! It's really enough to make me crazy."

"Really? Thank you! But, I've heard words like this hundreds of times."

Such an answer is very unsettling, but many too-good men do not think that these words have hurt themselves, and want to sincerely offer a hot heart; this heart must be placed in a gold-quality box and displayed on her dressing table, becoming her beloved treasure.

As for herself, she has long understood this very well. Since she is a prostitute, of course there will be all kinds of嫖客缠绕着 her around, unable to get rid of them, and there is no need to get rid of them. What they give her is the satisfaction of money, and what she gives them is the satisfaction of color and flesh. The exchange between each other is very reasonable. What's more, she has reached the age of maturity, so Master Zhang said that he must梳头 for her, so let him do it. Anyway, she will have to go through this once. Any man is a good opponent, it just depends on who can negotiate a good price with her old woman.

As for the background of Master Zhang, even Wu Gui does not understand it very well. It is said that he was indeed a candidate magistrate who would be released as soon as there was a vacancy, and his cousin was the current Daoyin. However, this has nothing to do with her, but what makes her most happy is that in addition to a pair of gold bracelets weighing three taels, there are also two very large pearls, which can be obtained immediately. She also wanted a gold necklace with a piece of green jade hanging in front, which would be very decent in front of others.

Regarding these things, after a few days of negotiations, because Master Zhang was very generous, everything was quickly settled completely, and waiting for the customized wooden furniture to be moved into her room, she could have a big lively celebration. The date has already been selected as the sixth day of March.

From then on, she was no longer a清官人. (To be continued)

Film Supplement

"Spring River Flower Moon Night" Overwhelms All Sound Films

— Si Ping

With the Gardens of Europe丨The Scenery of Switzerland as the Backdrop

With the Song Country of the World丨Famous Italian Melodies as the Core

Music, Singing, Mountain Light, Water Colors, Floral Fragrance, Poetic Charm, Romance丨All the beauty in the universe, all the beauty created by nature, can be said to be wonderfully captured in the "Spring River Flower Moon Night" that overwhelms all sound films. At a time when the American film industry is in decline, the Gaomeng Buleidian Film Company is able to grasp the characteristics of the European nation and create something unique, and this extraordinary success is worthy of our enthusiastic praise. The previous trend of European films not being welcomed can undoubtedly be changed by the artistry of "Spring River Flower Moon Night."

The direction, acting, cinematography, scenery, and sound recording of "Spring River Flower Moon Night"丨everything has succeeded to the point of perfection. The beauty of the music and the melodiousness of the singing are undoubtedly the characteristics of this film, and are beyond the reach of all other sound films. When we read a novel or a poem by a genius writer, we often appreciate it so much that we feel refreshed and transformed into a different person. We have the same aesthetic feeling after watching the film "Spring River Flower Moon Night". "Spring River Flower Moon Night" is a masterpiece that elevates the audience's tastes.

The plot of "Spring River Flower Moon Night" is very simple but its meaning is profound. The twists and turns of the story truly have the beauty of "mountains and rivers exhausted, yet another village appears." Its meaning is to depict the unrestrained genius丨the great Italian singer Fularle in the film丨as well as to satirize the ridiculous philistines丨the mayor Panteg in the film. All great literary masters, great poets, great artists, and great opera singers must have absolute freedom in order for their talents to be brought into full play. Talented people cannot rely on philistines, and philistines cannot restrain talented people; otherwise, talent will not be talent, and even if it is talent, it will be buried forever. In this film, the Italian genius singer Fularle is initially unhappy due to being constrained by a female manager. After he escapes midway, he encounters the mayor's entanglement, so he makes the best of the situation and even has his secretary replace him to avoid trouble! This is a depiction of a genius who does not care for fame but loves solitude.

This genius singer uses a "golden cicada shedding its shell" strategy, and the scene of him slowly closing the two large doors becomes a watershed for returning freedom. After that, he roams freely in the gardens of Europe丨at the foot of the mountains and on the shores of the waters of Switzerland. The film shows picturesque mountains and rivers. The beautiful rivers and mountains naturally become the home of genius. Even more poetic and romantic, he encounters a beautiful woman, and in a secluded corner where the mountains and waters meet, among a group of lively and innocent village children, this Italian singer sings loudly, unleashing his overflowing talent. Here, the clear mountains, beautiful waters, birdsong, and floral fragrance blend together seamlessly, and the audience will surely be intoxicated in this musicalized cinematic art. Italy is a world-renowned country of song. Although the songs of "Spring River Flower Moon Night" are recent works, the prelude of the film uses a radio broadcast to sing a long and melodious tune that is very pleasant to the ear. The melody of this song is used as a background music in the subsequent scenes. The second half of the film takes several unmatched songs from classical Italian opera, such as "Le Rêve" and "La Traviata," and sings them in succession through the voice of Kipra, culminating in "La Bohème," giving the audience the rare opportunity to enjoy three famous songs in one film. What's more, before this film, we also hear a symphony by the great German musician Beethoven.

Review of "Two Seconds"

— Ling He

Undoubtedly, this is a work that blurs the consciousness of the masses.

Construction worker John, after work, goes to a dance hall to have fun, where he meets a dancer, Xue Lan. In a drunken daze, he hastily marries her. Later, he also accidentally kills a good friend because of his anger at his wife's romantic behavior, and he himself is injured. When he is sick in bed, he is extremely poor and relies entirely on his wife for daily necessities. Because of his wife's confession, he learns that this money comes from her lover, and he is overwhelmed with shame and anger. But he luckily obtains a large sum of money, so he repays his wife's lover and kills him. Later, he surrenders himself to the court and serves his sentence.

Obviously, the screenwriter of this drama has put all his efforts into creating a typical worker who is steadfast, upright, and full of blood; and this worker must not recognize his own way out. Although he is in great pain due to his own economic oppression, he will not doubt whether the current social system is reasonable, and even when he is forced to commit murder, he is still determined to serve his sentence. Naturally, this kind of typical character is very beneficial to the people in the upper echelons of the organization. Therefore, in John's state of confused consciousness, there is actually a pastor who, under the condition that he has considerable income, proves that he does indeed have love for this dancer, and until the end, he does not even object to the existence of this marriage. Later, he loses his job due to illness, and although he is on the verge of desperation, he does not ask for compensation or medical expenses, and believes that love transcends everything and is ashamed of his wife's prostitution. At the time he owes money, he must pay it back, and if there is no way, he can "bet it all" on buying lottery tickets. (And he actually wins.) Of course, if you have money, you must pay back the money, pay back the money first and then kill someone. If you kill someone, you naturally have to serve your sentence without fear. And before you die, you should repent greatly. This is a "hero," this is a "good person" who is praised by gentlemen, and this is the best model for the working masses. Therefore, the screenwriter has created this very reasonable typical character on the screen, and this character is the best victim for maintaining modern laws.

As mentioned above, this typical character must become a preaching tool at the expense of many FILM conditions. But this is not an easy thing either. If you want to make a wide audience receive this kind of anaesthetic, then you must have good skills, and the acting and direction must be very moving. Regarding this point, it is precisely what the authors of "Two Seconds" have strived to achieve. They have faithfully fulfilled their "responsibilities."

The Educational Film Association Holds Its Second Annual Meeting

— Bai Hua

The Chinese Educational Film Association held its second annual meeting on the afternoon of the 5th of this month in the auditorium of the Ministry of Education on Chengxian Street in the capital. Members from various provinces were notified in advance to attend. Members from the Shanghai film industry who attended included Shao Zuiweng, Chen Yumei, and Li Yihe from Tianyi Company, Hong Shen and Zhou Jianyun from Mingxing Company, and Jin Qingyu from Lianhua Company. When the meeting began, it was chaired by Chu Minyi. Later, Chu left early due to important matters and was replaced by Duan Xipeng, the Deputy Minister of Education. After the chairman gave his speech, the general affairs, editing, and design groups reported on their work over the past year and distributed the association's publications, including: "Zengwu Report," narrated by Chen Lifu and noted by Wang Pingling, "New Lines for China's Film Industry," written by Sardi and translated by Peng Baichuan and Zhang Peiying, "Film and China," written by Chu Minyi, "Using Film to Promote the Realization of the Three Principles of the People and to Assist Various Undertakings," written by Sardi and translated by Peng Baichuan and Zhang Peiying, "An Overview of the Italian National Educational Film Museum." Next, Yin Zumao, a representative from the Central Party Headquarters, and Duan Xipeng, a representative from the Ministry of Education, gave speeches in succession. Then, Chen Lifu gave a speech. After the speech, it was late, and there was no time to discuss the proposals, so the meeting was adjourned and continued the next morning.

On the morning of the 6th, the meeting continued in the auditorium of the Ministry of Education. Chen Lifu, Peng Baichuan, Fang Zhi, and others proposed "Promoting the Safety of Domestic Films." Guo Youshou, Shao Zuiweng, Hong Shen, Zhou Jianyun, and Jin Qingyu were appointed to draft the proposal. Also, regarding the "Domestic Film Competition Case," it was decided to organize a selection committee, with members recommended by various agencies, including three from the Central Headquarters, one from the Academia Sinica, one from the Central University, two from the Ministry of Interior, two from the Ministry of Education, one from the Film Censorship Committee, and five from the Educational Film Association, totaling fifteen people. It was decided to screen the films on the 8th, with each committee member voting to select one sound film and one silent film. It is reported that the films participating in this competition are "Life Force" and "Two Orphans on the Battlefield" (both sound films) from Tianyi Company, and "Flower of Freedom" (sound film) and "Torrent" (silent film) from Mingxing Company, and "Humanity" (silent film) from Lianhua Company, totaling five films.

Introduction to "Life Force"

— Pan

"Life Force," recently completed and soon to be released by Tianyi Company, is a film with women as its subject. Its central consciousness has the following points: eradicating women's dependence on old habits; guiding women's path to struggle; encouraging women to develop a spirit of self-reliance; advocating for women to seek legitimate occupations; and at the same time, deeply and fully exposing the darkness of the current society and the coldness of human relationships. It is truly a good film that benefits society and women. The film will be released soon, and I, with the enthusiasm of supporting domestic films, am writing to introduce it.

The Secret of Film Novels (SECRETS) (4)

— Cairo

After some time, Mary was a young woman in a rural village in the American West. Little John had also been born. They lived in a small log cabin, divided into two small rooms, with a fireplace. The primitive-style furniture inside was all made by John himself. The cowhide on the dirt floor and the cradle where little John slept were also John's handiwork. Mary sometimes thought of her girlish life in New England, but she didn't feel any nostalgia or regret. She worshipped the real love life. She recognized that in the past, she only had empty fantasies about love, but now it was filled with sweetness and realized. She had John, and also little John.

She lay on little John's cradle, playing with little John. She said to him: "When you grow up in the future, you will be even greater than your father. Your father will be the governor of this province in the future, but you, you will be the president. Understand? The president."

As she was playing with little John like this, she suddenly heard the sound of horses' hooves in the distance outside the window. John and his assistant, called Shen Xiang, had gone to the neighboring village early that morning to buy food. Could they be back so soon? She listened again, and the sound of the horses' hooves got closer and closer. She ran to the door and opened it wide. Then her face sank. Three men with ferocious faces got off their horses. She took a few steps back in fear. The leader of the three stepped forward and said to Mary, "Hello, I am Jack Hauser, people call me 'Red-Faced Jack'. I'm afraid you've heard of me too."

Mary's face turned pale. She said, "I've heard of you."

"We've come to look for something to eat," the man said with a sneer.

"Don't waste your time, I have nothing, and I can't feed cattle thieves!" After she finished speaking, she pushed the door hard and locked it with an iron bolt. But when she was about to close that small window, a hairy hand had already reached in, and with a bang, a bullet had already flown past. Mary quickly ran over and hugged her child, who was still smiling. The robbers outside shouted, "We want something to eat, I advise you to open the door obediently." Mary hugged the child and slowly opened the door. Red-Faced Jack also introduced the other two: one was his brother, called Doufu, and the other was called Peter. They forced Mary to take out all the food. While they were gorging themselves, Doufu was constantly glancing at the beautiful woman in the countryside. But his appearance was noticed by Jack, who said, "Doufu, this time it's not allowed, you can come back next time."

After they finished eating, suddenly another person ran in and said to Jack: "Boss, the cows have all been rounded up." When Mary heard this, she jumped up and asked, "Cows? Whose cows?" (To be continued)
